What we care about is that\nrefactorings and `rope.base.change.Change`s use resources.\n\nThere are two options to create a `Resource` for a path in a project.\nNote that in these examples `path` is the path to a file or folder\nrelative to the project's root. A project's root folder is represented\nby an empty string.\n\n  1) Use the `rope.base.Project.get_resource()` method. E.g.:\n\n       myresource = myproject.get_resource(path)\n\n\n  2) Use the `rope.base.libutils` module. `libutils` has a function\n     named `path_to_resource()`. {"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_50","type":"agent_message","text":"The core issue I see is that the historical implementation used the resource’s `real_path` directly as the module element. That can be non-canonical for symlinked source roots, and it gives a package directory rather than the package’s executable `__init__.py`. I’m going to centralize that module-path choice in `libutils` and have codeassist use it."}}
